  <script nonce="UcfsBTuslF">
    window.globalExceptionHandler = function(err) {
      function reportToServer(errorObj) {
        function getCookie(cookie) {
          var value = "; " + document.cookie;
          var parts = value.split("; " + cookie + "=");
          if (parts.length == 2) {
            return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
          } else {
            return '';
          }
        }

        function serializeParam(data) {
          return Object.keys(data).map(function(key) {
            return key + '=' + encodeURIComponent(data[key]);
          }).join('&');
        }

        function _logToServer(data) {
          var BASE_REPORT_ERROR_URL = '/_/_/report/';
          var LOG_TYPE = 'error';
          var url = BASE_REPORT_ERROR_URL + LOG_TYPE + '/';
          var HTTP_METHOD = 'post';

          var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
          var csrfToken = getCookie('csrftoken');

          xhr.open(HTTP_METHOD, url, true);
          xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded');
          xhr.setRequestHeader('X-CSRFToken', csrfToken);
          xhr.send(serializeParam(data));
        }

        var reportContext = {
          current_url: window.location.href
        };

        var reportData;
        try {
          reportData = JSON.stringify({'errorObj': error});
        } catch (err) {
          var stringifyError = {
            'message': error.message,
            'name': 'window.onerror stringify exception'
          };
          reportData = JSON.stringify({
            'errorObj': stringifyError
          });
        }

        var xhrData = {
          report_context: JSON.stringify(reportContext),
          report_data: reportData,
        };

        _logToServer(xhrData);
      }

      var error = {};
      error.message = err.message || err.description;
      error.lineNumber = err.lineno || err.lineNumber || err.line;
      error.columnNumber = err.colno ||  err.columnNumber || err.column;
      error.stack = err.stack || err.stacktrace ||
        (err.error && (err.error.stack || err.error.stacktrace));
      error.fileName = err.fileName || err.sourceUrl;
      error.name = 'window.onerror';

      if (window.storeDispatchError) {
        window.storeDispatchError(error);
      } else {
        reportToServer(error);
      }
    }

    window.addEventListener('error', window.globalExceptionHandler);
  </script> 
  <script nonce="UcfsBTuslF">
    var onImageLoad = function(event) {
      if (!window.pwtTempStorage) {
        window.pwtTempStorage = {};
      }

      var tgt = event.target;
      var dataImagePrefix = 'data:image';
      if (tgt.tagName === 'IMG' && tgt.parentElement && tgt.parentElement.dataset &&
        tgt.parentElement.dataset.pwt === 'true') {
        var key = tgt.src && tgt.src.substr(0, dataImagePrefix.length) === dataImagePrefix ?
          tgt.src : tgt.src.split('/').pop();
        if (!window.pwtTempStorage[key]) {
          window.pwtTempStorage[key] = {
            time: window.performance.now(),
            visibility: window.getComputedStyle(tgt).visibility,
          };
        }
      }
    }

    if (window.performance && window.performance.now) {
      var calculateNumOfServerRenderedPinImages = function(event) {
        window.numOfServerRenderedPinImages = document.querySelectorAll('[data-pwt]').length;
      }

      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", calculateNumOfServerRenderedPinImages);
      document.body.addEventListener('load', onImageLoad, true);

      window.addEventListener('load', function() {
        document.body.removeEventListener('load', onImageLoad, true);
        document.removeEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', calculateNumOfServerRenderedPinImages);
      });
    }
  </script>
